It's a one-bedroom apartment that's been arranged as a hotel room. The bedroom, of course, has a bed and closet, and the "living room" has two queen beds and a chest of drawers with a tv on it. I would say it functions well as a crashpad, but after a long day of walking at Disneyland, I wanted to sit in a chair and relax so I went down to the parking garage and sat in my car. We used the airbed. Sheets were provided for the airbed, but there was no blanket for the airbed. I contacted the host about that during our stay but never heard back. Eventually I bought a blanket at Target. The three real beds are very low to the floor--could be difficult for some people to stand up from. The airbed is a tall airbed, but does lose some air overnight. Overall, our stay was okay, but we probably wouldn't do it again. It was pretty much exactly as the listing described, so read the listing carefully. There are no comforts of home here.
